2336         /**
2337          * Produces a VarHandle giving access to a static field {@code name} of
2338          * type {@code type} declared in a class of type {@code decl}.
2339          * The VarHandle's variable type is {@code type} and it has no
2340          * coordinate types.
2341          * <p>
2342          * Access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup
2343          * class.
2344          * <p>
2345          * If the returned VarHandle is operated on, the declaring class will be
2346          * initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2347          * <p>
2348          * Certain access modes of the returned VarHandle are unsupported under
2349          * the following conditions:
2350          * <ul>
2351          * <li>if the field is declared {@code final}, then the write, atomic
2352          *     update, numeric atomic update, and bitwise atomic update access
2353          *     modes are unsupported.
2354          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code byte},
2355          *     {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int}, {@code long},
2356          *     {@code float}, or {@code double}, then numeric atomic update
2357          *     access modes are unsupported.
2358          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code boolean},
2359          *     {@code byte}, {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int} or
2360          *     {@code long} then bitwise atomic update access modes are
2361          *     unsupported.
2362          * </ul>
2363          * <p>
2364          * If the field is declared {@code volatile} then the returned VarHandle
2365          * will override access to the field (effectively ignore the
2366          * {@code volatile} declaration) in accordance to its specified
2367          * access modes.
2368          * <p>
2369          * If the field type is {@code float} or {@code double} then numeric
2370          * and atomic update access modes compare values using their bitwise
2371          * representation (see {@link Float#floatToRawIntBits} and
2372          * {@link Double#doubleToRawLongBits}, respectively).
2373          * @apiNote
2374          * Bitwise comparison of {@code float} values or {@code double} values,
2375          * as performed by the numeric and atomic update access modes, differ
2376          * from the primitive {@code ==} operator and the {@link Float#equals}
2377          * and {@link Double#equals} methods, specifically with respect to
2378          * comparing NaN values or comparing {@code -0.0} with {@code +0.0}.
2379          * Care should be taken when performing a compare and set or a compare
2380          * and exchange operation with such values since the operation may
2381          * unexpectedly fail.
2382          * There are many possible NaN values that are considered to be
2383          * {@code NaN} in Java, although no IEEE 754 floating-point operation
2384          * provided by Java can distinguish between them.  Operation failure can
2385          * occur if the expected or witness value is a NaN value and it is
2386          * transformed (perhaps in a platform specific manner) into another NaN
2387          * value, and thus has a different bitwise representation (see
2388          * {@link Float#intBitsToFloat} or {@link Double#longBitsToDouble} for more
2389          * details).
2390          * The values {@code -0.0} and {@code +0.0} have different bitwise
2391          * representations but are considered equal when using the primitive
2392          * {@code ==} operator.  Operation failure can occur if, for example, a
2393          * numeric algorithm computes an expected value to be say {@code -0.0}
2394          * and previously computed the witness value to be say {@code +0.0}.
2395          * @param decl the class that declares the static field
2396          * @param name the field's name
2397          * @param type the field's type, of type {@code T}
2398          * @return a VarHandle giving access to a static field
2399          * @throws NoSuchFieldException if the field does not exist
2400          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails, or if the field is not {@code static}
2401          * @throws    SecurityException if a security manager is present and it
2402          *                              <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">refuses access</a>
2403          * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
2404          * @since 9
2405          */
2406         public VarHandle findStaticVarHandle(Class<?> decl, String name, Class<?> type) throws NoSuchFieldException, IllegalAccessException {
2407             MemberName getField = resolveOrFail(REF_getStatic, decl, name, type);
2408             MemberName putField = resolveOrFail(REF_putStatic, decl, name, type);
2409             return getFieldVarHandle(REF_getStatic, REF_putStatic, decl, getField, putField);
2410         }
2411 
2412         /**
2413          * Produces an early-bound method handle for a non-static method.
2414          * The receiver must have a supertype {@code defc} in which a method
2415          * of the given name and type is accessible to the lookup class.
2416          * The method and all its argument types must be accessible to the lookup object.
2417          * The type of the method handle will be that of the method,
2418          * without any insertion of an additional receiver parameter.
2419          * The given receiver will be bound into the method handle,
2420          * so that every call to the method handle will invoke the
2421          * requested method on the given receiver.
2422          * <p>
2423          * The returned method handle will have
2424          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2425          * the method's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set
2426          * <em>and</em> the trailing array argument is not the only argument.
2427          * (If the trailing array argument is the only argument,
2428          * the given receiver value will be bound to it.)
2429          * <p>
2430          * This is almost equivalent to the following code, with some differences noted below:
2431          * <blockquote><pre>{@code
2432 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
2433 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
2434 ...
2435 MethodHandle mh0 = lookup().findVirtual(defc, name, type);
2436 MethodHandle mh1 = mh0.bindTo(receiver);
2437 mh1 = mh1.withVarargs(mh0.isVarargsCollector());
2438 return mh1;
2439          * }</pre></blockquote>
2440          * where {@code defc} is either {@code receiver.getClass()} or a super
2441          * type of that class, in which the requested method is accessible
2442          * to the lookup class.
2443          * (Unlike {@code bind}, {@code bindTo} does not preserve variable arity.
2444          * Also, {@code bindTo} may throw a {@code ClassCastException} in instances where {@code bind} would
2445          * throw an {@code IllegalAccessException}, as in the case where the member is {@code protected} and
2446          * the receiver is restricted by {@code findVirtual} to the lookup class.)
2447          * @param receiver the object from which the method is accessed
2448          * @param name the name of the method
2449          * @param type the type of the method, with the receiver argument omitted
2450          * @return the desired method handle
2451          * @throws NoSuchMethodException if the method does not exist
2452          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2453          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2454          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2455          * @throws    SecurityException if a security manager is present and it
2456          *                              <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">refuses access</a>
2457          * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
2458          * @see MethodHandle#bindTo
2459          * @see #findVirtual
2460          */
2461         public MethodHandle bind(Object receiver, String name, MethodType type) throws NoSuchMethodException, IllegalAccessException {
2462             Class<? extends Object> refc = receiver.getClass(); // may get NPE
2463             MemberName method = resolveOrFail(REF_invokeSpecial, refc, name, type);
2464             MethodHandle mh = getDirectMethodNoRestrictInvokeSpecial(refc, method, findBoundCallerLookup(method));
2465             if (!mh.type().leadingReferenceParameter().isAssignableFrom(receiver.getClass())) {
2466                 throw new IllegalAccessException("The restricted defining class " +
2467                                                  mh.type().leadingReferenceParameter().getName() +
2468                                                  " is not assignable from receiver class " +
2469                                                  receiver.getClass().getName());
2470             }
2471             return mh.bindArgumentL(0, receiver).setVarargs(method);
2472         }
2473 
2474         /**
2475          * Makes a <a href="MethodHandleInfo.html#directmh">direct method handle</a>
2476          * to <i>m</i>, if the lookup class has permission.
2477          * If <i>m</i> is non-static, the receiver argument is treated as an initial argument.
2478          * If <i>m</i> is virtual, overriding is respected on every call.
2479          * Unlike the Core Reflection API, exceptions are <em>not</em> wrapped.
2480          * The type of the method handle will be that of the method,
2481          * with the receiver type prepended (but only if it is non-static).
2482          * If the method's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2483          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2484          * If <i>m</i> is not public, do not share the resulting handle with untrusted parties.
2485          * <p>
2486          * The returned method handle will have
2487          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2488          * the method's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set.
2489          * <p>
2490          * If <i>m</i> is static, and
2491          * if the returned method handle is invoked, the method's class will
2492          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2493          * @param m the reflected method
2494          * @return a method handle which can invoke the reflected method
2495          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2496          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2497          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2498          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2499          */
2500         public MethodHandle unreflect(Method m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2501             if (m.getDeclaringClass() == MethodHandle.class) {
2502                 MethodHandle mh = unreflectForMH(m);
2503                 if (mh != null)  return mh;
2504             }
2505             if (m.getDeclaringClass() == VarHandle.class) {
2506                 MethodHandle mh = unreflectForVH(m);
2507                 if (mh != null)  return mh;
2508             }
2509             MemberName method = new MemberName(m);
2510             byte refKind = method.getReferenceKind();
2511             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial)
2512                 refKind = REF_invokeVirtual;
2513             assert(method.isMethod());
2514             @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
2515             Lookup lookup = m.isAccessible() ? IMPL_LOOKUP : this;
2516             return lookup.getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(refKind, method.getDeclaringClass(), method, findBoundCallerLookup(method));
2517         }
2518         private MethodHandle unreflectForMH(Method m) {
2519             // these names require special lookups because they throw UnsupportedOperationException
2520             if (MemberName.isMethodHandleInvokeName(m.getName()))
2521                 return MethodHandleImpl.fakeMethodHandleInvoke(new MemberName(m));
2522             return null;
2523         }
2524         private MethodHandle unreflectForVH(Method m) {
2525             // these names require special lookups because they throw UnsupportedOperationException
2526             if (MemberName.isVarHandleMethodInvokeName(m.getName()))
2527                 return MethodHandleImpl.fakeVarHandleInvoke(new MemberName(m));
2528             return null;
2529         }
2530 
2531         /**
2532          * Produces a method handle for a reflected method.
2533          * It will bypass checks for overriding methods on the receiver,
2534          * <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#equiv">as if called</a> from an {@code invokespecial}
2535          * instruction from within the explicitly specified {@code specialCaller}.
2536          * The type of the method handle will be that of the method,
2537          * with a suitably restricted receiver type prepended.
2538          * (The receiver type will be {@code specialCaller} or a subtype.)
2539          * If the method's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2540          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class,
2541          * as if {@code invokespecial} instruction were being linked.
2542          * <p>
2543          * Before method resolution,
2544          * if the explicitly specified caller class is not identical with the
2545          * lookup class, or if this lookup object does not have
2546          * <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#privacc">private access</a>
2547          * privileges, the access fails.
2548          * <p>
2549          * The returned method handle will have
2550          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2551          * the method's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set.
2552          * @param m the reflected method
2553          * @param specialCaller the class nominally calling the method
2554          * @return a method handle which can invoke the reflected method
2555          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails,
2556          *                                or if the method is {@code static},
2557          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2558          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2559          * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
2560          */
2561         public MethodHandle unreflectSpecial(Method m, Class<?> specialCaller) throws IllegalAccessException {
2562             checkSpecialCaller(specialCaller, m.getDeclaringClass());
2563             Lookup specialLookup = this.in(specialCaller);
2564             MemberName method = new MemberName(m, true);
2565             assert(method.isMethod());
2566             // ignore m.isAccessible:  this is a new kind of access
2567             return specialLookup.getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(REF_invokeSpecial, method.getDeclaringClass(), method, findBoundCallerLookup(method));
2568         }
2569 
2570         /**
2571          * Produces a method handle for a reflected constructor.
2572          * The type of the method handle will be that of the constructor,
2573          * with the return type changed to the declaring class.
2574          * The method handle will perform a {@code newInstance} operation,
2575          * creating a new instance of the constructor's class on the
2576          * arguments passed to the method handle.
2577          * <p>
2578          * If the constructor's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2579          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2580          * <p>
2581          * The returned method handle will have
2582          * {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector variable arity} if and only if
2583          * the constructor's variable arity modifier bit ({@code 0x0080}) is set.
2584          * <p>
2585          * If the returned method handle is invoked, the constructor's class will
2586          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2587          * @param c the reflected constructor
2588          * @return a method handle which can invoke the reflected constructor
2589          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2590          *                                or if the method's variable arity modifier bit
2591          *                                is set and {@code asVarargsCollector} fails
2592          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2593          */
2594         public MethodHandle unreflectConstructor(Constructor<?> c) throws IllegalAccessException {
2595             MemberName ctor = new MemberName(c);
2596             assert(ctor.isObjectConstructorOrStaticInitMethod());
2597             @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
2598             Lookup lookup = c.isAccessible() ? IMPL_LOOKUP : this;
2599             if (ctor.isObjectConstructor()) {
2600                 assert(ctor.getReturnType() == void.class);
2601                 return lookup.getDirectConstructorNoSecurityManager(ctor.getDeclaringClass(), ctor);
2602             } else {
2603                 // static init factory is a static method
2604                 assert(ctor.isMethod() && ctor.getReturnType() == ctor.getDeclaringClass() && ctor.getReferenceKind() == REF_invokeStatic);
2605                 assert(!MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(ctor));  // must not be caller-sensitive
2606                 return lookup.getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(ctor.getReferenceKind(), ctor.getDeclaringClass(), ctor, lookup);
2607             }
2608         }
2609 
2610         /**
2611          * Produces a method handle giving read access to a reflected field.
2612          * The type of the method handle will have a return type of the field's
2613          * value type.
2614          * If the field is {@code static}, the method handle will take no arguments.
2615          * Otherwise, its single argument will be the instance containing
2616          * the field.
2617          * If the {@code Field} object's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2618          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2619          * <p>
2620          * If the field is static, and
2621          * if the returned method handle is invoked, the field's class will
2622          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2623          * @param f the reflected field
2624          * @return a method handle which can load values from the reflected field
2625          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2626          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2627          */
2628         public MethodHandle unreflectGetter(Field f) throws IllegalAccessException {
2629             return unreflectField(f, false);
2630         }
2631 
2632         /**
2633          * Produces a method handle giving write access to a reflected field.
2634          * The type of the method handle will have a void return type.
2635          * If the field is {@code static}, the method handle will take a single
2636          * argument, of the field's value type, the value to be stored.
2637          * Otherwise, the two arguments will be the instance containing
2638          * the field, and the value to be stored.
2639          * If the {@code Field} object's {@code accessible} flag is not set,
2640          * access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup class.
2641          * <p>
2642          * If the field is {@code final}, write access will not be
2643          * allowed and access checking will fail, except under certain
2644          * narrow circumstances documented for {@link Field#set Field.set}.
2645          * A method handle is returned only if a corresponding call to
2646          * the {@code Field} object's {@code set} method could return
2647          * normally.  In particular, fields which are both {@code static}
2648          * and {@code final} may never be set.
2649          * <p>
2650          * If the field is {@code static}, and
2651          * if the returned method handle is invoked, the field's class will
2652          * be initialized, if it has not already been initialized.
2653          * @param f the reflected field
2654          * @return a method handle which can store values into the reflected field
2655          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails,
2656          *         or if the field is {@code final} and write access
2657          *         is not enabled on the {@code Field} object
2658          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2659          */
2660         public MethodHandle unreflectSetter(Field f) throws IllegalAccessException {
2661             return unreflectField(f, true);
2662         }
2663 
2664         private MethodHandle unreflectField(Field f, boolean isSetter) throws IllegalAccessException {
2665             MemberName field = new MemberName(f, isSetter);
2666             if (isSetter && field.isStatic() && field.isFinal())
2667                 throw field.makeAccessException("static final field has no write access", this);
2668             assert(isSetter
2669                     ? MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsSetter(field.getReferenceKind())
2670                     : MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsGetter(field.getReferenceKind()));
2671             @SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
2672             Lookup lookup = f.isAccessible() ? IMPL_LOOKUP : this;
2673             return lookup.getDirectFieldNoSecurityManager(field.getReferenceKind(), f.getDeclaringClass(), field);
2674         }
2675 
2676         /**
2677          * Produces a VarHandle giving access to a reflected field {@code f}
2678          * of type {@code T} declared in a class of type {@code R}.
2679          * The VarHandle's variable type is {@code T}.
2680          * If the field is non-static the VarHandle has one coordinate type,
2681          * {@code R}.  Otherwise, the field is static, and the VarHandle has no
2682          * coordinate types.
2683          * <p>
2684          * Access checking is performed immediately on behalf of the lookup
2685          * class, regardless of the value of the field's {@code accessible}
2686          * flag.
2687          * <p>
2688          * If the field is static, and if the returned VarHandle is operated
2689          * on, the field's declaring class will be initialized, if it has not
2690          * already been initialized.
2691          * <p>
2692          * Certain access modes of the returned VarHandle are unsupported under
2693          * the following conditions:
2694          * <ul>
2695          * <li>if the field is declared {@code final}, then the write, atomic
2696          *     update, numeric atomic update, and bitwise atomic update access
2697          *     modes are unsupported.
2698          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code byte},
2699          *     {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int}, {@code long},
2700          *     {@code float}, or {@code double} then numeric atomic update
2701          *     access modes are unsupported.
2702          * <li>if the field type is anything other than {@code boolean},
2703          *     {@code byte}, {@code short}, {@code char}, {@code int} or
2704          *     {@code long} then bitwise atomic update access modes are
2705          *     unsupported.
2706          * </ul>
2707          * <p>
2708          * If the field is declared {@code volatile} then the returned VarHandle
2709          * will override access to the field (effectively ignore the
2710          * {@code volatile} declaration) in accordance to its specified
2711          * access modes.
2712          * <p>
2713          * If the field type is {@code float} or {@code double} then numeric
2714          * and atomic update access modes compare values using their bitwise
2715          * representation (see {@link Float#floatToRawIntBits} and
2716          * {@link Double#doubleToRawLongBits}, respectively).
2717          * @apiNote
2718          * Bitwise comparison of {@code float} values or {@code double} values,
2719          * as performed by the numeric and atomic update access modes, differ
2720          * from the primitive {@code ==} operator and the {@link Float#equals}
2721          * and {@link Double#equals} methods, specifically with respect to
2722          * comparing NaN values or comparing {@code -0.0} with {@code +0.0}.
2723          * Care should be taken when performing a compare and set or a compare
2724          * and exchange operation with such values since the operation may
2725          * unexpectedly fail.
2726          * There are many possible NaN values that are considered to be
2727          * {@code NaN} in Java, although no IEEE 754 floating-point operation
2728          * provided by Java can distinguish between them.  Operation failure can
2729          * occur if the expected or witness value is a NaN value and it is
2730          * transformed (perhaps in a platform specific manner) into another NaN
2731          * value, and thus has a different bitwise representation (see
2732          * {@link Float#intBitsToFloat} or {@link Double#longBitsToDouble} for more
2733          * details).
2734          * The values {@code -0.0} and {@code +0.0} have different bitwise
2735          * representations but are considered equal when using the primitive
2736          * {@code ==} operator.  Operation failure can occur if, for example, a
2737          * numeric algorithm computes an expected value to be say {@code -0.0}
2738          * and previously computed the witness value to be say {@code +0.0}.
2739          * @param f the reflected field, with a field of type {@code T}, and
2740          * a declaring class of type {@code R}
2741          * @return a VarHandle giving access to non-static fields or a static
2742          * field
2743          * @throws IllegalAccessException if access checking fails
2744          * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
2745          * @since 9
2746          */
2747         public VarHandle unreflectVarHandle(Field f) throws IllegalAccessException {
2748             MemberName getField = new MemberName(f, false);
2749             MemberName putField = new MemberName(f, true);
2750             return getFieldVarHandleNoSecurityManager(getField.getReferenceKind(), putField.getReferenceKind(),
2751                                                       f.getDeclaringClass(), getField, putField);
2752         }
2753 
2754         /**
2755          * Cracks a <a href="MethodHandleInfo.html#directmh">direct method handle</a>
2756          * created by this lookup object or a similar one.
2757          * Security and access checks are performed to ensure that this lookup object
2758          * is capable of reproducing the target method handle.
2759          * This means that the cracking may fail if target is a direct method handle
2760          * but was created by an unrelated lookup object.
2761          * This can happen if the method handle is <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#callsens">caller sensitive</a>
2762          * and was created by a lookup object for a different class.
2763          * @param target a direct method handle to crack into symbolic reference components
2764          * @return a symbolic reference which can be used to reconstruct this method handle from this lookup object
2765          * @throws    SecurityException if a security manager is present and it
2766          *                              <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">refuses access</a>
2767          * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the target is not a direct method handle or if access checking fails
2768          * @throws    NullPointerException if the target is {@code null}
2769          * @see MethodHandleInfo
2770          * @since 1.8
2771          */
2772         public MethodHandleInfo revealDirect(MethodHandle target) {
2773             MemberName member = target.internalMemberName();
2774             if (member == null || (!member.isResolved() &&
2775                                    !member.isMethodHandleInvoke() &&
2776                                    !member.isVarHandleMethodInvoke()))
2777                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("not a direct method handle");
2778             Class<?> defc = member.getDeclaringClass();
2779             byte refKind = member.getReferenceKind();
2780             assert(MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsValid(refKind));
2781             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial && !target.isInvokeSpecial())
2782                 // Devirtualized method invocation is usually formally virtual.
2783                 // To avoid creating extra MemberName objects for this common case,
2784                 // we encode this extra degree of freedom using MH.isInvokeSpecial.
2785                 refKind = REF_invokeVirtual;
2786             if (refKind == REF_invokeVirtual && defc.isInterface())
2787                 // Symbolic reference is through interface but resolves to Object method (toString, etc.)
2788                 refKind = REF_invokeInterface;
2789             // Check SM permissions and member access before cracking.
2790             try {
2791                 checkAccess(refKind, defc, member);
2792                 checkSecurityManager(defc, member);
2793             } catch (IllegalAccessException ex) {
2794                 throw new IllegalArgumentException(ex);
2795             }
2796             if (allowedModes != TRUSTED && member.isCallerSensitive()) {
2797                 Class<?> callerClass = target.internalCallerClass();
2798                 if (!hasFullPrivilegeAccess() || callerClass != lookupClass())
2799                     throw new IllegalArgumentException("method handle is caller sensitive: "+callerClass);
2800             }
2801             // Produce the handle to the results.
2802             return new InfoFromMemberName(this, member, refKind);
2803         }
2804 
2805         /// Helper methods, all package-private.
2806 
2807         MemberName resolveOrFail(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, String name, Class<?> type) throws NoSuchFieldException, IllegalAccessException {
2808             checkSymbolicClass(refc);  // do this before attempting to resolve
2809             Objects.requireNonNull(name);
2810             Objects.requireNonNull(type);
2811             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrFail(refKind, new MemberName(refc, name, type, refKind), lookupClassOrNull(),
2812                                             NoSuchFieldException.class);
2813         }
2814 
2815         MemberName resolveOrFail(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, String name, MethodType type) throws NoSuchMethodException, IllegalAccessException {
2816             checkSymbolicClass(refc);  // do this before attempting to resolve
2817             Objects.requireNonNull(name);
2818             Objects.requireNonNull(type);
2819             checkMethodName(refKind, name);  // NPE check on name
2820             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrFail(refKind, new MemberName(refc, name, type, refKind), lookupClassOrNull(),
2821                                             NoSuchMethodException.class);
2822         }
2823 
2824         MemberName resolveOrFail(byte refKind, MemberName member) throws ReflectiveOperationException {
2825             checkSymbolicClass(member.getDeclaringClass());  // do this before attempting to resolve
2826             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getName());
2827             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getType());
2828             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrFail(refKind, member, lookupClassOrNull(),
2829                                             ReflectiveOperationException.class);
2830         }
2831 
2832         MemberName resolveOrNull(byte refKind, MemberName member) {
2833             // do this before attempting to resolve
2834             if (!isClassAccessible(member.getDeclaringClass())) {
2835                 return null;
2836             }
2837             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getName());
2838             Objects.requireNonNull(member.getType());
2839             return IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrNull(refKind, member, lookupClassOrNull());
2840         }
2841 
2842         void checkSymbolicClass(Class<?> refc) throws IllegalAccessException {
2843             if (!isClassAccessible(refc)) {
2844                 throw new MemberName(refc).makeAccessException("symbolic reference class is not accessible", this);
2845             }
2846         }
2847 
2848         boolean isClassAccessible(Class<?> refc) {
2849             Objects.requireNonNull(refc);
2850             Class<?> caller = lookupClassOrNull();
2851             return caller == null || VerifyAccess.isClassAccessible(refc, caller, prevLookupClass, allowedModes);
2852         }
2853 
2854         /** Check name for an illegal leading "&lt;" character. */
2855         void checkMethodName(byte refKind, String name) throws NoSuchMethodException {
2856             // "<init>" can only be invoked via invokespecial or it's a static init factory
2857             if (name.startsWith("<") && refKind != REF_newInvokeSpecial &&
2858                     !(refKind == REF_invokeStatic && name.equals("<init>"))) {
2859                     throw new NoSuchMethodException("illegal method name: " + name);
2860             }
2861         }
2862 
2863         /**
2864          * Find my trustable caller class if m is a caller sensitive method.
2865          * If this lookup object has full privilege access, then the caller class is the lookupClass.
2866          * Otherwise, if m is caller-sensitive, throw IllegalAccessException.
2867          */
2868         Lookup findBoundCallerLookup(MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2869             if (MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(m) && !hasFullPrivilegeAccess()) {
2870                 // Only lookups with full privilege access are allowed to resolve caller-sensitive methods
2871                 throw new IllegalAccessException("Attempt to lookup caller-sensitive method using restricted lookup object");
2872             }
2873             return this;
2874         }
2875 
2876         /**
2877          * Returns {@code true} if this lookup has {@code PRIVATE} and {@code MODULE} access.
2878          * @return {@code true} if this lookup has {@code PRIVATE} and {@code MODULE} access.
2879          *
2880          * @deprecated This method was originally designed to test {@code PRIVATE} access
2881          * that implies full privilege access but {@code MODULE} access has since become
2882          * independent of {@code PRIVATE} access.  It is recommended to call
2883          * {@link #hasFullPrivilegeAccess()} instead.
2884          * @since 9
2885          */
2886         @Deprecated(since="14")
2887         public boolean hasPrivateAccess() {
2888             return hasFullPrivilegeAccess();
2889         }
2890 
2891         /**
2892          * Returns {@code true} if this lookup has <em>full privilege access</em>,
2893          * i.e. {@code PRIVATE} and {@code MODULE} access.
2894          * A {@code Lookup} object must have full privilege access in order to
2895          * access all members that are allowed to the {@linkplain #lookupClass() lookup class}.
2896          *
2897          * @return {@code true} if this lookup has full privilege access.
2898          * @since 14
2899          * @see <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#privacc">private and module access</a>
2900          */
2901         public boolean hasFullPrivilegeAccess() {
2902             return (allowedModes & (PRIVATE|MODULE)) == (PRIVATE|MODULE);
2903         }
2904 
2905         /**
2906          * Perform necessary <a href="MethodHandles.Lookup.html#secmgr">access checks</a>.
2907          * Determines a trustable caller class to compare with refc, the symbolic reference class.
2908          * If this lookup object has full privilege access, then the caller class is the lookupClass.
2909          */
2910         void checkSecurityManager(Class<?> refc, MemberName m) {
2911             if (allowedModes == TRUSTED)  return;
2912 
2913             SecurityManager smgr = System.getSecurityManager();
2914             if (smgr == null)  return;
2915 
2916             // Step 1:
2917             boolean fullPowerLookup = hasFullPrivilegeAccess();
2918             if (!fullPowerLookup ||
2919                 !VerifyAccess.classLoaderIsAncestor(lookupClass, refc)) {
2920                 ReflectUtil.checkPackageAccess(refc);
2921             }
2922 
2923             if (m == null) {  // findClass or accessClass
2924                 // Step 2b:
2925                 if (!fullPowerLookup) {
2926                     smgr.checkPermission(SecurityConstants.GET_CLASSLOADER_PERMISSION);
2927                 }
2928                 return;
2929             }
2930 
2931             // Step 2a:
2932             if (m.isPublic()) return;
2933             if (!fullPowerLookup) {
2934                 smgr.checkPermission(SecurityConstants.CHECK_MEMBER_ACCESS_PERMISSION);
2935             }
2936 
2937             // Step 3:
2938             Class<?> defc = m.getDeclaringClass();
2939             if (!fullPowerLookup && defc != refc) {
2940                 ReflectUtil.checkPackageAccess(defc);
2941             }
2942         }
2943 
2944         void checkMethod(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2945             boolean wantStatic = (refKind == REF_invokeStatic);
2946             String message;
2947             if (m.isObjectConstructor())
2948                 message = "expected a method, not a constructor";
2949             else if (!m.isMethod())
2950                 message = "expected a method";
2951             else if (wantStatic != m.isStatic())
2952                 message = wantStatic ? "expected a static method" : "expected a non-static method";
2953             else
2954                 { checkAccess(refKind, refc, m); return; }
2955             throw m.makeAccessException(message, this);
2956         }
2957 
2958         void checkField(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2959             boolean wantStatic = !MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(refKind);
2960             String message;
2961             if (wantStatic != m.isStatic())
2962                 message = wantStatic ? "expected a static field" : "expected a non-static field";
2963             else
2964                 { checkAccess(refKind, refc, m); return; }
2965             throw m.makeAccessException(message, this);
2966         }
2967 
2968         /** Check public/protected/private bits on the symbolic reference class and its member. */
2969         void checkAccess(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName m) throws IllegalAccessException {
2970             assert(m.referenceKindIsConsistentWith(refKind) &&
2971                    MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsValid(refKind) &&
2972                    (MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsField(refKind) == m.isField()));
2973             int allowedModes = this.allowedModes;
2974             if (allowedModes == TRUSTED)  return;
2975             int mods = m.getModifiers();
2976             if (Modifier.isProtected(mods) &&
2977                     refKind == REF_invokeVirtual &&
2978                     m.getDeclaringClass() == Object.class &&
2979                     m.getName().equals("clone") &&
2980                     refc.isArray()) {
2981                 // The JVM does this hack also.
2982                 // (See ClassVerifier::verify_invoke_instructions
2983                 // and LinkResolver::check_method_accessability.)
2984                 // Because the JVM does not allow separate methods on array types,
2985                 // there is no separate method for int[].clone.
2986                 // All arrays simply inherit Object.clone.
2987                 // But for access checking logic, we make Object.clone
2988                 // (normally protected) appear to be public.
2989                 // Later on, when the DirectMethodHandle is created,
2990                 // its leading argument will be restricted to the
2991                 // requested array type.
2992                 // N.B. The return type is not adjusted, because
2993                 // that is *not* the bytecode behavior.
2994                 mods ^= Modifier.PROTECTED | Modifier.PUBLIC;
2995             }
2996             if (Modifier.isProtected(mods) && refKind == REF_newInvokeSpecial) {
2997                 // cannot "new" a protected ctor in a different package
2998                 mods ^= Modifier.PROTECTED;
2999             }
3000             if (Modifier.isFinal(mods) &&
3001                     MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsSetter(refKind))
3002                 throw m.makeAccessException("unexpected set of a final field", this);
3003             int requestedModes = fixmods(mods);  // adjust 0 => PACKAGE
3004             if ((requestedModes & allowedModes) != 0) {
3005                 if (VerifyAccess.isMemberAccessible(refc, m.getDeclaringClass(),
3006                                                     mods, lookupClass(), previousLookupClass(), allowedModes))
3007                     return;
3008             } else {
3009                 // Protected members can also be checked as if they were package-private.
3010                 if ((requestedModes & PROTECTED) != 0 && (allowedModes & PACKAGE) != 0
3011                         && VerifyAccess.isSamePackage(m.getDeclaringClass(), lookupClass()))
3012                     return;
3013             }
3014             throw m.makeAccessException(accessFailedMessage(refc, m), this);
3015         }
3016 
3017         String accessFailedMessage(Class<?> refc, MemberName m) {
3018             Class<?> defc = m.getDeclaringClass();
3019             int mods = m.getModifiers();
3020             // check the class first:
3021             boolean classOK = (Modifier.isPublic(defc.getModifiers()) &&
3022                                (defc == refc ||
3023                                 Modifier.isPublic(refc.getModifiers())));
3024             if (!classOK && (allowedModes & PACKAGE) != 0) {
3025                 // ignore previous lookup class to check if default package access
3026                 classOK = (VerifyAccess.isClassAccessible(defc, lookupClass(), null, FULL_POWER_MODES) &&
3027                            (defc == refc ||
3028                             VerifyAccess.isClassAccessible(refc, lookupClass(), null, FULL_POWER_MODES)));
3029             }
3030             if (!classOK)
3031                 return "class is not public";
3032             if (Modifier.isPublic(mods))
3033                 return "access to public member failed";  // (how?, module not readable?)
3034             if (Modifier.isPrivate(mods))
3035                 return "member is private";
3036             if (Modifier.isProtected(mods))
3037                 return "member is protected";
3038             return "member is private to package";
3039         }
3040 
3041         private void checkSpecialCaller(Class<?> specialCaller, Class<?> refc) throws IllegalAccessException {
3042             int allowedModes = this.allowedModes;
3043             if (allowedModes == TRUSTED)  return;
3044             if ((lookupModes() & PRIVATE) == 0
3045                 || (specialCaller != lookupClass()
3046                        // ensure non-abstract methods in superinterfaces can be special-invoked
3047                     && !(refc != null && refc.isInterface() && refc.isAssignableFrom(specialCaller))))
3048                 throw new MemberName(specialCaller).
3049                     makeAccessException("no private access for invokespecial", this);
3050         }
3051 
3052         private boolean restrictProtectedReceiver(MemberName method) {
3053             // The accessing class only has the right to use a protected member
3054             // on itself or a subclass.  Enforce that restriction, from JVMS 5.4.4, etc.
3055             if (!method.isProtected() || method.isStatic()
3056                 || allowedModes == TRUSTED
3057                 || method.getDeclaringClass() == lookupClass()
3058                 || VerifyAccess.isSamePackage(method.getDeclaringClass(), lookupClass()))
3059                 return false;
3060             return true;
3061         }
3062         private MethodHandle restrictReceiver(MemberName method, DirectMethodHandle mh, Class<?> caller) throws IllegalAccessException {
3063             assert(!method.isStatic());
3064             // receiver type of mh is too wide; narrow to caller
3065             if (!method.getDeclaringClass().isAssignableFrom(caller)) {
3066                 throw method.makeAccessException("caller class must be a subclass below the method", caller);
3067             }
3068             MethodType rawType = mh.type();
3069             if (caller.isAssignableFrom(rawType.parameterType(0))) return mh; // no need to restrict; already narrow
3070             MethodType narrowType = rawType.changeParameterType(0, caller);
3071             assert(!mh.isVarargsCollector());  // viewAsType will lose varargs-ness
3072             assert(mh.viewAsTypeChecks(narrowType, true));
3073             return mh.copyWith(narrowType, mh.form);
3074         }
3075 
3076         /** Check access and get the requested method. */
3077         private MethodHandle getDirectMethod(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName method, Lookup callerLookup) throws IllegalAccessException {
3078             final boolean doRestrict    = true;
3079             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3080             return getDirectMethodCommon(refKind, refc, method, checkSecurity, doRestrict, callerLookup);
3081         }
3082         /** Check access and get the requested method, for invokespecial with no restriction on the application of narrowing rules. */
3083         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodNoRestrictInvokeSpecial(Class<?> refc, MemberName method, Lookup callerLookup) throws IllegalAccessException {
3084             final boolean doRestrict    = false;
3085             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3086             return getDirectMethodCommon(REF_invokeSpecial, refc, method, checkSecurity, doRestrict, callerLookup);
3087         }
3088         /** Check access and get the requested method, eliding security manager checks. */
3089         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName method, Lookup callerLookup) throws IllegalAccessException {
3090             final boolean doRestrict    = true;
3091             final boolean checkSecurity = false;  // not needed for reflection or for linking CONSTANT_MH constants
3092             return getDirectMethodCommon(refKind, refc, method, checkSecurity, doRestrict, callerLookup);
3093         }
3094         /** Common code for all methods; do not call directly except from immediately above. */
3095         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodCommon(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName method,
3096                                                    boolean checkSecurity,
3097                                                    boolean doRestrict,
3098                                                    Lookup boundCaller) throws IllegalAccessException {
3099             checkMethod(refKind, refc, method);
3100             // Optionally check with the security manager; this isn't needed for unreflect* calls.
3101             if (checkSecurity)
3102                 checkSecurityManager(refc, method);
3103             assert(!method.isMethodHandleInvoke());
3104 
3105             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial &&
3106                 refc != lookupClass() &&
3107                 !refc.isInterface() &&
3108                 refc != lookupClass().getSuperclass() &&
3109                 refc.isAssignableFrom(lookupClass())) {
3110                 assert(!method.getName().equals("<init>"));  // not this code path
3111 
3112                 // Per JVMS 6.5, desc. of invokespecial instruction:
3113                 // If the method is in a superclass of the LC,
3114                 // and if our original search was above LC.super,
3115                 // repeat the search (symbolic lookup) from LC.super
3116                 // and continue with the direct superclass of that class,
3117                 // and so forth, until a match is found or no further superclasses exist.
3118                 // FIXME: MemberName.resolve should handle this instead.
3119                 Class<?> refcAsSuper = lookupClass();
3120                 MemberName m2;
3121                 do {
3122                     refcAsSuper = refcAsSuper.getSuperclass();
3123                     m2 = new MemberName(refcAsSuper,
3124                                         method.getName(),
3125                                         method.getMethodType(),
3126                                         REF_invokeSpecial);
3127                     m2 = IMPL_NAMES.resolveOrNull(refKind, m2, lookupClassOrNull());
3128                 } while (m2 == null &&         // no method is found yet
3129                          refc != refcAsSuper); // search up to refc
3130                 if (m2 == null)  throw new InternalError(method.toString());
3131                 method = m2;
3132                 refc = refcAsSuper;
3133                 // redo basic checks
3134                 checkMethod(refKind, refc, method);
3135             }
3136             DirectMethodHandle dmh = DirectMethodHandle.make(refKind, refc, method, lookupClass());
3137             MethodHandle mh = dmh;
3138             // Optionally narrow the receiver argument to lookupClass using restrictReceiver.
3139             if ((doRestrict && refKind == REF_invokeSpecial) ||
3140                     (MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(refKind) && restrictProtectedReceiver(method))) {
3141                 mh = restrictReceiver(method, dmh, lookupClass());
3142             }
3143             mh = maybeBindCaller(method, mh, boundCaller);
3144             mh = mh.setVarargs(method);
3145             return mh;
3146         }
3147         private MethodHandle maybeBindCaller(MemberName method, MethodHandle mh, Lookup boundCaller)
3148                                              throws IllegalAccessException {
3149             if (boundCaller.allowedModes == TRUSTED || !MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(method))
3150                 return mh;
3151 
3152             // boundCaller must have full privilege access.
3153             // It should have been checked by findBoundCallerLookup. Safe to check this again.
3154             if (!boundCaller.hasFullPrivilegeAccess())
3155                 throw new IllegalAccessException("Attempt to lookup caller-sensitive method using restricted lookup object");
3156 
3157             MethodHandle cbmh = MethodHandleImpl.bindCaller(mh, boundCaller.lookupClass);
3158             // Note: caller will apply varargs after this step happens.
3159             return cbmh;
3160         }
3161 
3162         /** Check access and get the requested field. */
3163         private MethodHandle getDirectField(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName field) throws IllegalAccessException {
3164             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3165             return getDirectFieldCommon(refKind, refc, field, checkSecurity);
3166         }
3167         /** Check access and get the requested field, eliding security manager checks. */
3168         private MethodHandle getDirectFieldNoSecurityManager(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName field) throws IllegalAccessException {
3169             final boolean checkSecurity = false;  // not needed for reflection or for linking CONSTANT_MH constants
3170             return getDirectFieldCommon(refKind, refc, field, checkSecurity);
3171         }
3172         /** Common code for all fields; do not call directly except from immediately above. */
3173         private MethodHandle getDirectFieldCommon(byte refKind, Class<?> refc, MemberName field,
3174                                                   boolean checkSecurity) throws IllegalAccessException {
3175             checkField(refKind, refc, field);
3176             // Optionally check with the security manager; this isn't needed for unreflect* calls.
3177             if (checkSecurity)
3178                 checkSecurityManager(refc, field);
3179             DirectMethodHandle dmh = DirectMethodHandle.make(refc, field);
3180             boolean doRestrict = (MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(refKind) &&
3181                                     restrictProtectedReceiver(field));
3182             if (doRestrict)
3183                 return restrictReceiver(field, dmh, lookupClass());
3184             return dmh;
3185         }
3186         private VarHandle getFieldVarHandle(byte getRefKind, byte putRefKind,
3187                                             Class<?> refc, MemberName getField, MemberName putField)
3188                 throws IllegalAccessException {
3189             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3190             return getFieldVarHandleCommon(getRefKind, putRefKind, refc, getField, putField, checkSecurity);
3191         }
3192         private VarHandle getFieldVarHandleNoSecurityManager(byte getRefKind, byte putRefKind,
3193                                                              Class<?> refc, MemberName getField, MemberName putField)
3194                 throws IllegalAccessException {
3195             final boolean checkSecurity = false;
3196             return getFieldVarHandleCommon(getRefKind, putRefKind, refc, getField, putField, checkSecurity);
3197         }
3198         private VarHandle getFieldVarHandleCommon(byte getRefKind, byte putRefKind,
3199                                                   Class<?> refc, MemberName getField, MemberName putField,
3200                                                   boolean checkSecurity) throws IllegalAccessException {
3201             assert getField.isStatic() == putField.isStatic();
3202             assert getField.isGetter() && putField.isSetter();
3203             assert MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsStatic(getRefKind) == MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsStatic(putRefKind);
3204             assert MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsGetter(getRefKind) && MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsSetter(putRefKind);
3205 
3206             checkField(getRefKind, refc, getField);
3207             if (checkSecurity)
3208                 checkSecurityManager(refc, getField);
3209 
3210             if (!putField.isFinal()) {
3211                 // A VarHandle does not support updates to final fields, any
3212                 // such VarHandle to a final field will be read-only and
3213                 // therefore the following write-based accessibility checks are
3214                 // only required for non-final fields
3215                 checkField(putRefKind, refc, putField);
3216                 if (checkSecurity)
3217                     checkSecurityManager(refc, putField);
3218             }
3219 
3220             boolean doRestrict = (MethodHandleNatives.refKindHasReceiver(getRefKind) &&
3221                                   restrictProtectedReceiver(getField));
3222             if (doRestrict) {
3223                 assert !getField.isStatic();
3224                 // receiver type of VarHandle is too wide; narrow to caller
3225                 if (!getField.getDeclaringClass().isAssignableFrom(lookupClass())) {
3226                     throw getField.makeAccessException("caller class must be a subclass below the method", lookupClass());
3227                 }
3228                 refc = lookupClass();
3229             }
3230             boolean isWriteAllowedOnFinalFields = this.allowedModes == TRUSTED;
3231             return VarHandles.makeFieldHandle(getField, refc, getField.getFieldType(), isWriteAllowedOnFinalFields);
3232         }
3233         /** Check access and get the requested constructor. */
3234         private MethodHandle getDirectConstructor(Class<?> refc, MemberName ctor) throws IllegalAccessException {
3235             final boolean checkSecurity = true;
3236             return getDirectConstructorCommon(refc, ctor, checkSecurity);
3237         }
3238         /** Check access and get the requested constructor, eliding security manager checks. */
3239         private MethodHandle getDirectConstructorNoSecurityManager(Class<?> refc, MemberName ctor) throws IllegalAccessException {
3240             final boolean checkSecurity = false;  // not needed for reflection or for linking CONSTANT_MH constants
3241             return getDirectConstructorCommon(refc, ctor, checkSecurity);
3242         }
3243         /** Common code for all constructors; do not call directly except from immediately above. */
3244         private MethodHandle getDirectConstructorCommon(Class<?> refc, MemberName ctor,
3245                                                   boolean checkSecurity) throws IllegalAccessException {
3246             assert(ctor.isObjectConstructor());
3247             checkAccess(REF_newInvokeSpecial, refc, ctor);
3248             // Optionally check with the security manager; this isn't needed for unreflect* calls.
3249             if (checkSecurity)
3250                 checkSecurityManager(refc, ctor);
3251             assert(!MethodHandleNatives.isCallerSensitive(ctor));  // maybeBindCaller not relevant here
3252             return DirectMethodHandle.make(ctor).setVarargs(ctor);
3253         }
3254 
3255         /** Hook called from the JVM (via MethodHandleNatives) to link MH constants:
3256          */
3257         /*non-public*/
3258         MethodHandle linkMethodHandleConstant(byte refKind, Class<?> defc, String name, Object type)
3259                 throws ReflectiveOperationException {
3260             if (!(type instanceof Class || type instanceof MethodType))
3261                 throw new InternalError("unresolved MemberName");
3262             MemberName member = new MemberName(refKind, defc, name, type);
3263             MethodHandle mh = LOOKASIDE_TABLE.get(member);
3264             if (mh != null) {
3265                 checkSymbolicClass(defc);
3266                 return mh;
3267             }
3268             if (defc == MethodHandle.class && refKind == REF_invokeVirtual) {
3269                 // Treat MethodHandle.invoke and invokeExact specially.
3270                 mh = findVirtualForMH(member.getName(), member.getMethodType());
3271                 if (mh != null) {
3272                     return mh;
3273                 }
3274             } else if (defc == VarHandle.class && refKind == REF_invokeVirtual) {
3275                 // Treat signature-polymorphic methods on VarHandle specially.
3276                 mh = findVirtualForVH(member.getName(), member.getMethodType());
3277                 if (mh != null) {
3278                     return mh;
3279                 }
3280             }
3281             MemberName resolved = resolveOrFail(refKind, member);
3282             mh = getDirectMethodForConstant(refKind, defc, resolved);
3283             if (mh instanceof DirectMethodHandle
3284                     && canBeCached(refKind, defc, resolved)) {
3285                 MemberName key = mh.internalMemberName();
3286                 if (key != null) {
3287                     key = key.asNormalOriginal();
3288                 }
3289                 if (member.equals(key)) {  // better safe than sorry
3290                     LOOKASIDE_TABLE.put(key, (DirectMethodHandle) mh);
3291                 }
3292             }
3293             return mh;
3294         }
3295         private boolean canBeCached(byte refKind, Class<?> defc, MemberName member) {
3296             if (refKind == REF_invokeSpecial) {
3297                 return false;
3298             }
3299             if (!Modifier.isPublic(defc.getModifiers()) ||
3300                     !Modifier.isPublic(member.getDeclaringClass().getModifiers()) ||
3301                     !member.isPublic() ||
3302                     member.isCallerSensitive()) {
3303                 return false;
3304             }
3305             ClassLoader loader = defc.getClassLoader();
3306             if (loader != null) {
3307                 ClassLoader sysl = ClassLoader.getSystemClassLoader();
3308                 boolean found = false;
3309                 while (sysl != null) {
3310                     if (loader == sysl) { found = true; break; }
3311                     sysl = sysl.getParent();
3312                 }
3313                 if (!found) {
3314                     return false;
3315                 }
3316             }
3317             try {
3318                 MemberName resolved2 = publicLookup().resolveOrNull(refKind,
3319                     new MemberName(refKind, defc, member.getName(), member.getType()));
3320                 if (resolved2 == null) {
3321                     return false;
3322                 }
3323                 checkSecurityManager(defc, resolved2);
3324             } catch (SecurityException ex) {
3325                 return false;
3326             }
3327             return true;
3328         }
3329         private MethodHandle getDirectMethodForConstant(byte refKind, Class<?> defc, MemberName member)
3330                 throws ReflectiveOperationException {
3331             if (MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsField(refKind)) {
3332                 return getDirectFieldNoSecurityManager(refKind, defc, member);
3333             } else if (MethodHandleNatives.refKindIsMethod(refKind)) {
3334                 return getDirectMethodNoSecurityManager(refKind, defc, member, findBoundCallerLookup(member));
3335             } else if (refKind == REF_newInvokeSpecial) {
3336                 return getDirectConstructorNoSecurityManager(defc, member);
3337             }
3338             // oops
3339             throw newIllegalArgumentException("bad MethodHandle constant #"+member);
3340         }
3341 
3342         static ConcurrentHashMap<MemberName, DirectMethodHandle> LOOKASIDE_TABLE = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
3343     }
3344 
3345     /**
3346      * Produces a method handle constructing arrays of a desired type,
3347      * as if by the {@code anewarray} bytecode.
3348      * The return type of the method handle will be the array type.
3349      * The type of its sole argument will be {@code int}, which specifies the size of the array.
3350      *
3351      * <p> If the returned method handle is invoked with a negative
3352      * array size, a {@code NegativeArraySizeException} will be thrown.
3353      *
3354      * @param arrayClass an array type
3355      * @return a method handle which can create arrays of the given type
3356      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is {@code null}
3357      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code arrayClass} is not an array type
3358      * @see java.lang.reflect.Array#newInstance(Class, int)
3359      * @jvms 6.5 {@code anewarray} Instruction
3360      * @since 9
3361      */
3362     public static MethodHandle arrayConstructor(Class<?> arrayClass) throws IllegalArgumentException {
3363         if (!arrayClass.isArray()) {
3364             throw newIllegalArgumentException("not an array class: " + arrayClass.getName());
3365         }
3366         MethodHandle ani = MethodHandleImpl.getConstantHandle(MethodHandleImpl.MH_Array_newInstance).
3367                 bindTo(arrayClass.getComponentType());
3368         return ani.asType(ani.type().changeReturnType(arrayClass));
3369     }

3371     /**
3372      * Produces a method handle returning the length of an array,
3373      * as if by the {@code arraylength} bytecode.
3374      * The type of the method handle will have {@code int} as return type,
3375      * and its sole argument will be the array type.
3376      *
3377      * <p> If the returned method handle is invoked with a {@code null}
3378      * array reference, a {@code NullPointerException} will be thrown.
3379      *
3380      * @param arrayClass an array type
3381      * @return a method handle which can retrieve the length of an array of the given array type
3382      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is {@code null}
3383      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if arrayClass is not an array type
3384      * @jvms 6.5 {@code arraylength} Instruction
3385      * @since 9
3386      */
3387     public static MethodHandle arrayLength(Class<?> arrayClass) throws IllegalArgumentException {
3388         return MethodHandleImpl.makeArrayElementAccessor(arrayClass, MethodHandleImpl.ArrayAccess.LENGTH);
3389     }

3391     /**
3392      * Produces a method handle giving read access to elements of an array,
3393      * as if by the {@code aaload} bytecode.
3394      * The type of the method handle will have a return type of the array's
3395      * element type.  Its first argument will be the array type,
3396      * and the second will be {@code int}.
3397      *
3398      * <p> When the returned method handle is invoked,
3399      * the array reference and array index are checked.
3400      * A {@code NullPointerException} will be thrown if the array reference
3401      * is {@code null} and an {@code ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException} will be
3402      * thrown if the index is negative or if it is greater than or equal to
3403      * the length of the array.
3404      *
3405      * @param arrayClass an array type
3406      * @return a method handle which can load values from the given array type
3407      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
3408      * @throws  IllegalArgumentException if arrayClass is not an array type
3409      * @jvms 6.5 {@code aaload} Instruction
3410      */
3411     public static MethodHandle arrayElementGetter(Class<?> arrayClass) throws IllegalArgumentException {
3412         return MethodHandleImpl.makeArrayElementAccessor(arrayClass, MethodHandleImpl.ArrayAccess.GET);
3413     }
